<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:излечивать.html>изле́чивать</a> (23666)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:излечить.html>излечи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izlečítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:излечивать.html>изле́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izléčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:излечить.html>излечи́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изливать.html>излива́ть</a> (27325)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:излить.html>изли́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izlítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изливать.html>излива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izlivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:излить.html>изли́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pour out, to vent (emotions, etc.)</li></ol>

***изливаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изливаться.html>излива́ться</a> (26903)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изливать.html>излива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izlivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изливаться.html>излива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izlivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изли́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spill out, to pour out, to flow out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to radiate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of light, sound, or smell</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to manifest, to appear <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + prepositional, in a specified way; of feelings, moods, or experiences</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнев.html>гнев</a> <b>изли́лся</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:резкий.html>ре́зких</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gnev <b>izlílsja</b> v rézkix slováx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">anger <b>manifested</b> in sharp words</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pour one's heart out</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изливать.html>излива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izlivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">litʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***излишний.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:излишний.html>изли́шний</a> (4863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:излишний.html>изли́шний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izlíšnij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>superfluous</li>
<li>unnecessary</li>
<li>excessive</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изловить.html>излови́ть</a> (17245)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изловить.html>излови́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izlovítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">by chasing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полиция.html>поли́ция</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:производить.html>производи́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повальный.html>пова́льные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обыск.html>о́быски</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изловить.html>излови́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сотня.html>со́тни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:продажный.html>прода́жных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщин</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Polícija proizvodíla poválʹnyje óbyski i <b>izlovíla</b> bóleje sótni prodážnyx žénščin</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Police conducted searches en masse and <b>caught</b> more than a hundred corrupt women</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:увидеть.html>уви́дите</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловко.html>ло́вко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изловить.html>изловлю́</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vy uvídite, kak lóvko ja jevó <b>izlovljú</b>!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You will see how shrewdly I will <b>catch</b> him/it!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изложение.html>изложе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izložénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изложение.html>изложе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изложение.html>изложе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изложение.html>изложе́ний</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изложить.html>изложи́ть</a> (4483)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изложить.html>изложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izložítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:излагать.html>излага́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:излом.html>изло́м</a> (20209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***излучать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:излучать.html>излуча́ть</a> (14315)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">излучи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izlučítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:излучать.html>излуча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izlučátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">излучи́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to radiate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:излучать.html>излуча́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дость</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:уверенность.html>уве́ренность</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izlučátʹ</b> rádostʹ (uvérennostʹ)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to radiate happiness (confidence)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мазать.html>ма́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mázatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измазать.html>изма́зать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmázatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изма́зывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make dirty, to smear
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Александр Солженицын, <i>Матрёнин <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двор</a></i> 1968:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Матрёна <a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гала</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:среди.html>среди́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужчина.html>мужчи́н</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:суетиться.html>суети́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помогать.html>помога́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:накатывать.html>нака́тывать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бревно.html>брёвна</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сани.html>са́ни</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>Тут</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заметить.html>заме́тил</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мое́й</a>  <a href = vnd.unilang:телогрейка.html>телогре́йке</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:измазать.html>изма́зала</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рукав.html>рукава́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:льдистый.html>льди́стую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>грязь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бревно.html>брёвен</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Matrjóna bégala sredí mužčín, sujetílasʹ i pomogála nakátyvatʹ brjóvna na sáni. Tut zamétil ja, što oná v mojéj  telogréjke, užé <b>izmázala</b> rukavá o lʹdístuju grjazʹ brjóven</i></dd><dd>Matryona ran among the men, chitchatted and helped rolling logs up to the sleigh, whereupon I noticed she was wearing my padded jacket and had already <b>smeared</b> its sleeves with the logs' iced dirt</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изматывать.html>изма́тываемый</a> (29110)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изматывать.html>изма́тываемый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmátyvajemyj</span>)
</p>

***измельчать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:измельчать.html>измельча́ть</a> (31987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измельчить.html>измельчи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izmelʹčítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измельчать.html>измельча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmelʹčátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измельчить.html>измельчи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crumble up, to chop, to crush, to pound, to grind
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:измельчать.html>измельча́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кора.html>кору́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izmelʹčátʹ</b> korú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to chop the bark</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:измельчать.html>измельча́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порошок.html>порошо́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izmelʹčátʹ</b> v porošók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to powder, reduce to powder</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мельчи́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">melʹčítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мельча́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">melʹčátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измельчать.html>измельча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmelʹčátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мельча́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become small/smaller</li>
<li>to become petty, to degenerate</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>ме́лкий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mélkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>ме́лко</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mélko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ме́льче</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mélʹče</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
